# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Cell membrane ^XKevhHPt

Transports hot water by interfacing with the cell membrane ^77yzXwFb

Crystalline insulator  ^6a5GQKN3

ATP storage module ^LXDLRDfg

Atp carrier protein  ^9FInTD9T

Waste carrier protein that carries filtered waste to the lysosome  ^1TH37tY0

Problem and Solution ^3wIk7hnd

Many cells are faced with harsh temperature conditions especially heat, to
combat this the Colorwandle takes in heat energy in the form of water by
interfacing with the cell membrane and then converts uses the temperature 
of that water to create ATP energy and waste product which is transported
to the lysosome using proteins while the ATP is also transported using ATP
carrier proteins. ^fgwVilHm

Calorwandle ^bfJ3jaW5

German for change ^GGxktOCx

Latin for heat ^X4lRPiIb

Pros and cons ^dqX9SlWj

The benefits are that the organell combats 
the adverse effects of heat and turns that 
con into an advantage by creating energy. 
The organell however could also cause 
instability by introducing to much waste to
the lysosome creating a domino effect 
exponentially building up waste inside of the
cell. ^OiXdn5AX
